<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:right;margin:0pt;"><b>Exhibit 99.1 </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:center;margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>iCAD Reports Financial Results for First Quarter Ended March 31, 2023</b>&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: center;">Company to host conference call and webcast today at 4:30 PM ET&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt;">NASHUA, N.H. &#8211; May 15, 2022 &#8211; iCAD, Inc. (NASDAQ: ICAD),&#8239;a global medical technology leader providing innovative cancer detection and therapy solutions, today reported its financial and operating results for the three months ended March 31, 2023.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Highlights: </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">

		<tr>
			<td style="width:34pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top;width:18pt;">
			<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top;">
			<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Body of evidence supporting iCAD&#8217;s technologies grows, with compelling new research supporting Company&#8217;s Breast AI Suite and Xoft presented at key industry tradeshows and published in peer-reviewed journals</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">

		<tr>
			<td style="width:34pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top;width:18pt;">
			<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top;">
			<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Leadership team strengthened with seasoned executives poised to accelerate key initiatives in the Company&#8217;s strategic expansion</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">

		<tr>
			<td style="width:34pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top;width:18pt;">
			<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top;">
			<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Company implemented a number of strategic changes, including continued cost reduction measures to align and streamline cost base, reducing annualized expenses by $4.3 - $4.6 million and annualized cash burn by $4.9 - $5.2 million, putting Company on track to achieve profitability exiting 2024</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt;">&#8220;We are making bold moves to rapidly transform this Company, with a focus on preserving cash and building a defensible and competitive long-term strategy that diversifies our revenue stream and smooths out our customer concentration. Demand for our technology continues to be strong and the body of evidence supporting it continues to grow, with compelling new research supporting ProFound AI Detection, ProFound AI Risk and the Xoft System published in peer-reviewed journals and presented at key industry tradeshows last quarter,&#8221; said Dana Brown, President and CEO of iCAD, Inc.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt;">&#8220;We are continuing to fortify our team with the addition of several seasoned executives who will accelerate key initiatives in the Company&#8217;s strategic plan, including forging new and strategic relationships that will ensure our continued success, such as partnerships with patient advocacy groups, pharmaceutical companies, and payer organizations. I am confident that their unique skillsets and contributions will be invaluable to our progress, as we work to scale the impact of our AI solutions and revolutionize patient care worldwide,&#8221; said Ms. Brown.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&#8220;With a continued focus on creating runway, preserving cash and building a defensible and competitive long-term strategy, we are currently going through a rigorous and thoughtful process to evaluate a range of growth opportunities to diversify our revenue stream and expand access to our technology to more customers and patients worldwide. I remain optimistic about the Company and its future, and I am confident that we are taking the right steps to ensure continued growth and create additional shareholder value,&#8221; said Ms. Brown.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Three Months Ended&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094326091">March 31, 2023</a></b><b> Financial Results </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a> was $5.8 million, a decrease of $1.7&nbsp;million, or 23%, as compared to the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Revenue: Cancer Detection revenue for the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a>, which includes the Company&#8217;s mammography and breast density products, and the associated service and supplies revenue, was $4.3&nbsp;million, a decrease of 22%, as compared to the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>. Therapy revenue for the&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a>, which includes Xoft&#174; Axxent&#174; eBx&#174; System&#174; sales, as well as the associated service and supplies revenue, was $1.4&nbsp;million, a decrease of 28%, as compared to the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Gross Profit: Gross profit for the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a> was $4.1&nbsp;million, or 71% of revenue, as compared to $5.3&nbsp;million, or 71% of revenue, in the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a> were $7.7&nbsp;million, a 12% decrease from $8.8&nbsp;million in the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">GAAP Net Loss: Net loss for the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a> was ($3.8) million, or ($0.15)&nbsp;per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($3.5) million, or ($0.14) per diluted share, for the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 27pt;">Non-GAAP Adjusted Net Loss: Non-GAAP Adjusted Net Loss, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined below, for the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a> was ($3.6) million, or ($0.14) per diluted share, as compared to a Non-GAAP Adjusted Net Loss of ($3.5) million, or ($0.14) per diluted share, for the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="6" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">first</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>. Please refer to the section entitled &#8220;Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#8221; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to Non-GAAP Adjusted Net Loss results for the three-month periods ended <a data-tblloc="7x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="6" id="led395579F20233211682094343599">March 31, 2023 and 2022</a>, respectively.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Use of Non-GAAP Financial Measures </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">In its quarterly news releases, conference calls, slide presentations or webcasts, the Company may use or discuss non-GAAP financial measures as defined by SEC Regulation G. The GAAP financial measures most directly comparable to each non-GAAP financial measure used or discussed, and a reconciliation of the differences between each non-GAAP financial measure and the comparable GAAP financial measure, are included in this press release after the condensed consolidated financial statements. When analyzing the Company&#8217;s operating performance, investors should not consider these non-GAAP measures as a substitute for the comparable financial measures prepared in accordance with GAAP. The Company&#8217;s quarterly news releases containing such non-GAAP reconciliations can be found on the Investors section of the Company&#8217;s website at www.icadmed.com.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">The Company reports its financial results in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles, or GAAP. However, management believes that in order to understand the Company&#8217;s short-term and long-term financial and operational trends, investors may wish to consider the impact of certain non-cash or non-recurring items, when used as a supplement to financial performance measures in accordance with GAAP. These items result from facts and circumstances that vary in frequency and/or impact on continuing operations. Management also uses results of operations before such items to evaluate the operating performance of the Company and compare it against past periods, make operating decisions, and serve as a basis for strategic planning. These non-GAAP financial measures provide management with additional means to understand and evaluate the operating results and trends in the Company&#8217;s ongoing business by eliminating certain non-cash expenses and other items that management believes might otherwise make comparisons of the Company&#8217;s ongoing business with prior periods more difficult, obscure trends in ongoing operations or reduce management&#8217;s ability to make useful forecasts. Management believes that these non-GAAP financial measures provide additional means of evaluating period-over-period operating performance. In addition, management understands that some investors and financial analysts find this information helpful in analyzing the Company&#8217;s financial and operational performance and comparing this performance to its peers and competitors.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Management defines &#8220;Non-GAAP Adjusted EBITDA&#8221; as the sum of GAAP Net Loss before provisions for interest expense, other income, stock-based compensation expense, depreciation and amortization, tax expense, severance, gain on sale of assets, loss on disposal of assets, acquisition and litigation related expenses. Management considers this non-GAAP financial measure to be an indicator of the Company&#8217;s operational strength and performance of its business and a good measure of its historical operating trends, in particular the extent to which ongoing operations impact the Company&#8217;s overall financial performance.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">The non-GAAP financial measures do not replace the presentation of the Company&#8217;s GAAP financial results and should only be used as a supplement to, not as a substitute for, the Company&#8217;s financial results presented in accordance with GAAP. The Company has provided a reconciliation of each non-GAAP financial measure used in its financial reporting and investor presentations to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Management excludes each of the items identified below from the applicable non-GAAP financial measure referenced above for the reasons set forth with respect to that excluded item:</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Interest expense: The Company excludes interest expense which includes interest from the facility agreement, interest on capital leases and interest on the convertible debentures from its non-GAAP Adjusted EBITDA calculation.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Stock-based compensation expense: excluded as these are non-cash expenses that management does not consider part of ongoing operating results when assessing the performance of the Company&#8217;s business, and also because the total amount of expense is partially outside of the Company&#8217;s control as it is based on factors such as stock price volatility and interest rates, which may be unrelated to our performance during the period in which the expense is incurred.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Amortization and Depreciation: Purchased assets and intangibles are amortized over a period of several years and generally cannot be changed or influenced by management after they are acquired. Accordingly, these non-cash items are not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such expenses do not have a direct correlation to future business operations. Thus, including such charges does not accurately reflect the performance of the Company&#8217;s ongoing operations for the period in which such charges are incurred.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Severance and Furlough: The Company has incurred severance and furlough expenses in connection with restructuring and in connection with the separation of its former CEO.&nbsp; The Company excludes these items from its non-GAAP financial measures when evaluating its continuing business performance as such&nbsp;items can vary significantly and do not reflect expected future operating expenses. In addition, management believes that such items do not have a direct correlation to future business operations.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Loss on fair value of convertible debentures. The Company excludes this non-cash item as it is not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Litigation related: These expenses consist primarily of settlement, legal and other professional fees related to litigation. The Company excludes these costs from its non-GAAP measures primarily because the Company believes that these costs have no direct correlation to the core operations of the Company.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>

			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;font-size: 10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Loss on extinguishment of debt: The Company excludes this non-cash item as it is not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">On occasion in the future, there may be other items, such as loss on extinguishment of debt, significant asset impairments, restructuring charges or significant gains or losses from contingencies that the Company may exclude if it believes that doing so is consistent with the goal of providing useful information to investors and management.</p>
